<w:left w:w="240" w:type="dxa"/><w:bottom w:w="150" w:type="dxa"/><w:right w:w="0" w:type="dxa"/></w:tcMar><w:vAlign w:val="center"/><w:hideMark/></w:tcPr><w:p w14:paraId="65486BDF" w14:textId="77777777" w:rsidR="006B1243" w:rsidRPr="006B1243" w:rsidRDefault="006B1243" w:rsidP="006B1243"><w:r w:rsidRPr="006B1243">8.5/10 → Production-Grade
1. Executive Summary
TravelMate is a trust-first group travel matching platform designed to connect verified strangers with compatible travel preferences, enabling safe and enjoyable group trips. The platform positions 
safety as an architectural constraint
—not a bolt-on feature—with identity verification (Aadhaar/DigiLocker/KYC) as the foundational layer that gates access to matching.
Market Context:
 The global travel companion matching services market was valued at 
$1.8 billion in 2025** and is expected to reach **$4.7 billion by 2034
 at an 11.2% CAGR. India's travel technology market is rapidly growing, driven by increasing internet penetration, smartphone adoption, and a growing middle-class population.
Problem Statement:
 Solo travelers and small groups struggle to find compatible, trustworthy travel companions. Existing solutions lack robust identity verification, meaningful compatibility matching, and safety infrastructure—particularly for women travelers.
Solution:
 A mobile-first platform combining:
Government ID-based identity verification (Aadhaar/DigiLocker via Setu/Surepass/IDfy)
Multi-stage matching pipeline with constrained optimization
Women-only groups and gender-preference hard filters
In-trip safety features (SOS, live location sharing, trip buddy pairing)
Post-trip two-way ratings with bad-actor flagging
Event-driven architecture for scalability
2. Production-Ready Architecture Enhancements

3. Problem Definition (Formal)
3.1 Objective Function
Maximize average pairwise compatibility within each group, subject to:
Group size 
∈
 [4, 8] (or user-specified range)
Same destination ± 0 (exact match required)
Date window overlap ≥ 2 days
Budget tier match (low/mid/high)
Verified identity (hard gate)
Gender-preference compatibility (hard constraint)
3.2 Constraints

Primary objective for MVP:
 
Group cohesion
 (maximize compatibility) with batch matching every 24-48 hours.
4. Improved Matching Pipeline
4.1 Pipeline Overview
text
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                         MATCHING PIPELINE                                  │
├
─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
┤
│                                                                             │
│  [1] DESTINATION FILTER                                                     │
│      └── Exact match required                                              │
│                                                                             │
│  [2] DATE WINDOW FILTER                                                    │
│      └── Minimum 2-day overlap required                                    │
│                                                                             │
│  [3] BUDGET FILTER                                                         │
│      └── Tier match required (low/mid/high)                                │
│                                                                             │
│  [4] GENDER PREFERENCE FILTER                                              │
│      └── Hard rejection on incompatibility                                 │
│                                                                             │
│  [5] AGE BUCKET PREFERENCE                                                 │
│      └── Soft preference; can be relaxed                                   │
│                                                                             │
│  [6] INTEREST EMBEDDING                                                    │
│      └── Convert tags to embedding vectors                                 │
│                                                                             │
│  [7] CANDIDATE POOL GENERATION                                             │
│      └── All users passing hard filters                                    │
│                                                                             │
│  [8] COMPATIBILITY GRAPH CONSTRUCTION                                      │
│      └── Weighted edges between candidates                                 │
│                                                                             │
│  [9] CONSTRAINED GROUP OPTIMIZER                                           │
│      └── Greedy packing + local swap optimization                          │
│                                                                             │
│  [10] GROUP FORMATION                                                      │
│      └── Groups of 4-8 users with max compatibility                        │
│                                                                             │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
4.2 Compatibility Score Formula
text
Score(A,B) = 
    0.30 × Date_Overlap +
    0.20 × Interest_Similarity +
    0.15 × Budget_Match +
    0.10 × Travel_Style_Compatibility +
    0.10 × Age_Compatibility +
    0.05 × Language_Compatibility +
    0.05 × Previous_Ratings_Avg +
    0.05 × Trust_Score
Where:
- Date_Overlap = (min(end_a, end_b) - max(start_a, start_b)) / total_days
- Interest_Similarity = Jaccard similarity of interest tags
- Budget_Match = 1.0 if same tier, 0.5 if adjacent, 0.0 otherwise
- Travel_Style_Compatibility = Cosine similarity of style vectors
- Age_Compatibility = 1 - (|age_a - age_b| / max_age_diff)
- Language_Compatibility = Jaccard of spoken languages
- Previous_Ratings_Avg = Average of user's past ratings (normalized 0-1)
- Trust_Score = Composite of verification status + social proof
4.3 Multi-Stage Filtering Benefits

12.3 Safety Features Pipeline
text
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                         SAFETY ARCHITECTURE                               │
├
─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
┤
│                                                                             │
│  [1] VERIFICATION GATE                                                     │
│      
├
──
 Phone OTP + Email                                                 
│
│      
├
──
 Aadhaar/DigiLocker KYC (store only reference)                    
│
│      └── Verified badge → Trust score boost                              │
│                                                                             │
│  [2] MATCHING FILTERS (Hard Constraints)                                   │
│      
├
──
 Gender preference hard rejection                                  
│
│      
├
──
 Verified-only visibility                                          
│
│      └── Trust score threshold (minimum for matching)                     │
│                                                                             │
│  [3] IN-TRIP SAFETY                                                        │
│      
├
──
 SOS button 
→
 Emergency contact + Police API                      
│
│      
├
──
 Live location sharing (opt-in, WebSocket)                        
│
│      └── "Trip buddy" pairing (accountability unit of 2)                  │
│                                                                             │
│  [4] POST-TRIP ACCOUNTABILITY                                              │
│      
├
──
 Blind two-way rating (prevents retaliation bias)                 
│
│      
├
──
 Flag/report 
→
 Risk engine analysis                               
│
│      └── Auto-removal from matching pool (if risk score exceeds threshold)│
│                                                                             │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
12.4 Women's Safety Specifics
Women-only group toggle
 at signup — segments matching pool
Verified-ID-only visibility
 — unverified users cannot match
AI-driven safety indicators
 (future) — ratings from female travelers, neighborhood safety
Emergency contact
 stored and accessible via SOS
13. Itinerary Generation
13.1 Approach: Rule-Based Template + LLM Personalization
MVP:
 Rule-based template engine
Day-wise template per destination (seeded manually for top destinations)
Deterministic logic for activity sequencing
Optimistic locking for collaborative editing
Future:
 LLM-powered personalization
Adapt to group's live feedback and preferences
Generate personalized descriptions and recommendations
13.2 Template Structure (Example: Manali)
text
Day 1: Arrival + Local Sightseeing
  - 10:00 AM: Check-in at hostel/hotel
  - 12:00 PM: Lunch (local cuisine recommendation)
  - 2:00 PM: Hadimba Temple visit
  - 4:00 PM: Mall Road shopping
  - 7:00 PM: Group dinner (optional)
Day 2: Adventure
  - 9:00 AM: Solang Valley → Paragliding/Zorbing
  - 1:00 PM: Packed lunch at valley
  - 3:00 PM: Return to Manali
  - Evening: Free time / group activity vote
Day 3: Departure
  - 9:00 AM: Breakfast
  - 11:00 AM: Check-out

16. Implementation Roadmap
Phase 1: Foundation (Weeks 1-3)
Project setup + tech stack selection
Database schema design + migration (all tables)
Authentication (phone OTP + email + JWT)
User profile CRUD (expanded schema)
Basic UI screens (signup, profile, home)
API Gateway setup (auth, rate limiting)
Observability foundation (metrics, logs, traces)
Phase 2: Matching Engine (Weeks 4-7)
Trip creation flow
Multi-stage filtering (destination + date + budget + gender)
Compatibility scoring function (normalized weights)
Constrained greedy packing + local swap optimization
UserCompatibility table for caching
Batch scheduler with distributed locking
Match notification via dedicated notification service
Phase 3: Safety &amp; Trust (Weeks 8-10)
KYC verification flow (mocked UI + documented integration)
Store only KYC provider references
Verified badge + trust score display
Gender-preference hard filter
Women-only toggle
Blind post-trip rating system
Flag/report functionality with risk engine
WebSocket group chat
Phase 4: Itinerary &amp; Guide (Weeks 10-12)
Static itinerary templates (5-10 destinations)
Optimistic locking for collaborative itinerary editing
Guide profile + request flow
Group view with member profiles + trust scores
Group lifecycle state machine
Polish + demo preparation
Phase 5: Documentation &amp; Presentation (Week 13)
System design diagrams (architecture, ERD, state machines)
API integration documentation
Safety architecture diagram
Limitations &amp; future scope section
Demo video / presentation
17. Future Roadmap (Won't Build Now)
